## Poland events by Matoro ##

add_namespace = poland_events
add_namespace = poland_flavour_events
add_namespace = poland_news_events

### Starting Events ###
country_event = { #The Emergency Session
	id = poland_events.5
	title = poland_events.5.t
	desc = poland_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_king

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.5 option poland_events.5.a"
		name = poland_events.5.a
		add_political_power = 50
		complete_national_focus = POL_Emergency_Session
	}
}

country_event = { #Future of the Privy Council
	id = poland_events.6
	title = poland_events.6.t
	desc = poland_events.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_royal_castle

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.6 option poland_events.6.a"
		name = poland_events.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ruler_traits = {
				remove = POL_geheimrat
				add = POL_geheimrat1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			var:country_leader = {
				clr_character_flag = POL_geheimrat
				set_character_flag = POL_geheimrat1
				set_temp_variable = { remove_trait_token = token:POL_geheimrat }
				set_temp_variable = { add_trait_token = token:POL_geheimrat1 }
				swap_traits_in_all_country_leader_roles = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.6 option poland_events.6.b"
		name = poland_events.6.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ruler_traits = {
				remove = POL_geheimrat
				add = POL_geheimrat2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			var:country_leader = {
				clr_character_flag = POL_geheimrat
				set_character_flag = POL_geheimrat2
				set_temp_variable = { remove_trait_token = token:POL_geheimrat }
				set_temp_variable = { add_trait_token = token:POL_geheimrat2 }
				swap_traits_in_all_country_leader_roles = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.6 option poland_events.6.c"
		name = poland_events.6.c
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ruler_traits = {
				remove = POL_geheimrat
				add = POL_geheimrat3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			var:country_leader = {
				clr_character_flag = POL_geheimrat
				set_character_flag = POL_geheimrat3
				set_temp_variable = { remove_trait_token = token:POL_geheimrat }
				set_temp_variable = { add_trait_token = token:POL_geheimrat3 }
				swap_traits_in_all_country_leader_roles = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #PPS's leadership
	id = poland_events.7
	title = poland_events.7.t
	desc = poland_events.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_PPS

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.7 option poland_events.7.a"
		name = poland_events.7.a #Barlicki
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				has_country_flag = POL_FRA_supported_dubois
				NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_AUS_supported_barlicki }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_GER }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -5 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_AUS_supported_barlicki }
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland_events.7.barlicki_tt2
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland_events.7.barlicki_tt1
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.7 option poland_events.7.b"
		name = poland_events.7.b #Dubois
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				has_country_flag = POL_AUS_supported_barlicki
				NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_FRA_supported_dubois }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_GER }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -10 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
		set_country_flag = POL_PPS_Dubois
		clr_country_flag = POL_PPS_Barlicki
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_FRA_supported_dubois }
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland_events.7.dubois_tt2
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland_events.7.dubois_tt1
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = poland_events.114
			FRA = { country_event = poland_events.114 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland_events.114 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Peasant unrest (prelude to the strike)
	id = poland_events.9
	title = poland_events.9.t
	desc = poland_events.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_peasant_revolt

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = poland_events.10 days = 46 } #Peasant strikes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_PPS_Dubois } }
				country_event = { id = poland_events.11 days = 52 } #PPS joins if pro-Rep
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = poland_events.13 days = 12 } } #inform GER
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.9 option poland_events.9.a"
		name = poland_events.9.a
		add_stability = -0.04
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.9 option poland_events.9.b"
		name = poland_events.9.b
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -4 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
	}
}

}

country_event = { #PPS Joins the Strike
	id = poland_events.11
	title = poland_events.11.t
	desc = poland_events.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_general_strike

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.11 option poland_events.11.a"
		name = poland_events.11.a
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.11
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -5 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -5 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.11 option poland_events.11.b"
		name = poland_events.11.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		add_political_power = -40
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = POL_labour_strikes2
			days = 60
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -3 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.12 option poland_events.12.b"

		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes

			random_list = {
				10 = { country_event = { id = poland_events.14 days = 3 } }
				20 = { country_event = { id = poland_events.16 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Peasants crushed
	id = poland_events.16
	title = poland_events.16.t
	desc = poland_events.16.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_peasant_unrest }
				remove_ideas = POL_peasant_unrest
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.16 option poland_events.16.a"
		name = poland_events.16.a
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_manpower = -345
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.06
		}
		remove_ideas = POL_great_peasant_strike
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -6 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.16 option poland_events.16.b"
		name = poland_events.16.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		remove_ideas = POL_great_peasant_strike
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -5 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
	}
}

	desc = poland_events.18.d

		hidden_effect = {

				limit = { has_idea = POL_peasant_unrest }

			}
			country_event = { id = poland_events.19 days = 365 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.18 option poland_events.18.a"

			ideology = social_liberal

##Underground events
country_event = { #Republicans smuggling from Galicia
	id = poland_events.22
	title = poland_events.22.t
	desc = poland_events.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_university_warsaw
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { owns_state = 88 }
		is_monarchy = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.22 option poland_events.22.a"
		name = poland_events.22.a
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_talks_with_galicia }
			GAL = { exists = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
				is_ai = no
			}
			country_event = poland_events.31
		}
		else = {
			GAL = { country_event = poland_events.31 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 4 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		set_country_flag = POL_talks_with_galicia
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.22 option poland_events.22.b"
		name = poland_events.22.b

#end the investigations
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.81
	title = poland_events.81.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_major_purge }
		text = poland_events.81.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_minor_purge }
		text = poland_events.81.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_no_purge }
		text = poland_events.81.d3
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_kingdom_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = POL_krakow_conspiracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 6
					has_country_flag = POL_army_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_bund_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_unions_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_church_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PPS
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PSL
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_chjena
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_major_purge
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					has_country_flag = POL_army_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_bund_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_unions_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_church_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PPS
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PSL
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_chjena
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_minor_purge
		}
		else = { set_country_flag = POL_no_purge }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.81 option poland_events.81.a"
		name = poland_events.81.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_major_purge }
			clr_country_flag = POL_major_purge
			add_ideas = POL_decimated_underground
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_minor_purge }
			clr_country_flag = POL_minor_purge
			add_ideas = POL_weakened_underground
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = POL_no_purge
				if = {
					limit = {
						POL = { is_ai = yes }
					}
					NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_NO_REVOLT } }
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = POL_no_purge
			add_ideas = POL_active_underground
		}
	}
}

#Party Popularity Surges!
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.118
	title = poland_events.118.t
	desc = poland_events.118.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.118 option poland_events.118.a"
		name = poland_events.118.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = FRA.POL_election_support }
			POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.02
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					5 = {
						POL = {
							set_country_flag = POL_fraud_PPS
							country_event = { id = poland_events.119 days = 5 }
						}
					}
					5 = { }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = RUS }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = RUS.POL_election_support }
			POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.06
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					5 = {
						POL = {
							set_country_flag = POL_fraud_chjena
							country_event = { id = poland_events.119 days = 5 }
						}
					}
					5 = { }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = AUS }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = AUS.POL_election_support }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					5 = {
						POL = {
							set_country_flag = POL_fraud_PSL
							country_event = { id = poland_events.119 days = 5 }
						}
					}
					5 = { }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = GER }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = GER.POL_election_support }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					5 = {
						POL = {
							set_country_flag = POL_fraud_circle
							country_event = { id = poland_events.119 days = 5 }
						}
					}
					5 = { }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = poland_events.119.d

	fire_only_once = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.119 option poland_events.119.a"
		name = poland_events.119.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					GER = { is_ai = no }
					AUS = { is_ai = no }
					RUS = { is_ai = no }
					FRA = { is_ai = no }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.03

			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_fraud_PPS }

		}

			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_fraud_chjena }

country_event = { #Elections of 1938
	id = poland_events.150
	title = poland_events.150.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_sejm

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { is_ai = yes } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_MARLIB }
				}
				set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 45 }
				set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 15 }
				set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 25 }
				set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 15 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
				}
				set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
				set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 20 }
				set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 20 }
				set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 45 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_AUTDEM }
				}
				set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 45 }
				set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 20 }
				set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 20 }
				set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 15 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_idea = POL_coalition_broken } }
						add_ideas = POL_coalition_broken
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_AUS }
						has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
				set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 45 }
				set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 15 }
				set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
						has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
				set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 15 }
				set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 45 }
				set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
						has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_GER }
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					seed = random
					10 = {
						set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
						set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 45 }
						set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 15 }
						set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
					}
					10 = {
						set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
						set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 15 }
						set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 45 }
						set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = poland_events.150.d.circle_coalition
		trigger = {

			NOT = { has_idea = POL_coalition_broken }

#Election Victory for X
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.151
	title = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		text = poland_events.151.t.ci
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { has_government = social_conservative }
		text = poland_events.151.t.ch
	}
	title = {
		trigger = {
			has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
		}
		text = poland_events.151.t.ce
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		text = poland_events.151.d.ci
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_government = social_conservative }
		text = poland_events.151.d.ch
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
		}
		text = poland_events.151.d.ce
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_royal_castle

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = POL_coalition_broken
			remove_ideas = POL_sejm_dismissed
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.151 option poland_events.151.a.ci"

			OR = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}

#The King Appoints Studnicki
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.152
	title = poland_events.152.t
	desc = poland_events.152.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_studnicki

	trigger = {
		is_monarchy = yes
		OR = {
			has_country_leader = { character = POL_august_von_hohenzollern }
			has_country_leader = { character = POL_alexander_von_hohenzollern }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = POL_coalition_broken
			remove_ideas = POL_sejm_dismissed
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.152 option poland_events.152.a"
		name = poland_events.152.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_circle_real_victory } }
			add_political_power = -50
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -20 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -10 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		remove_from_coalition = yes

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}

		activate_advisor = POL_wladyslaw_studnicki_sic
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		complete_national_focus = POL_Election_of_1938
		clr_country_flag = POL_supported_jews
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = { id = germany_foreign_events_new.82 days = 10 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Elections of 1942
	id = poland_events.153
	title = poland_events.153.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_soccon_or_marlib_government = yes
		}
		text = poland_events.153.d.free
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_authdem_or_pataut_government = yes
		}
		text = poland_events.153.d.auth
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_sejm

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1939.01.01
		is_monarchy = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_second_monarchy_election }
	}
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = POL_second_monarchy_election
		end_coalition = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.153 option poland_events.153.a"
		name = poland_events.153.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_royal_influence > 40 }
			NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_royal_influence > 50 } }
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 10 }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 5 }
		}
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = market_liberal }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		}
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.08
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.153 option poland_events.153.b"
		name = poland_events.153.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_AUTDEM }
					has_completed_focus = POL_Entrenched_Constitutionalism
					has_completed_focus = POL_Constitutionalist_Coalition
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = market_liberal } }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.04 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = social_conservative } }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.04 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -5 }
		POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.153 option poland_events.153.c"
		name = poland_events.153.c
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = POL_Entrenched_Constitutionalism }

				factor = 0

					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_AUTDEM }

			}
		}

		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -5 }

		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
	}

	id = poland_events.197

		OR = {
			POL = { is_ai = no }
			AND = {
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_socialist_uprising }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_nationalist_uprising }
		is_monarchy = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.197 option poland_events.197.a"
		name = poland_events.197.a
		add_stability = -0.15
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = poland_events.198 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland_events.199 }
			country_event = { id = poland_events.200 days = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						GER_is_du_path = yes
						has_country_flag = GER_polish_list_not_happy_flag
					}
				}
				GER = { country_event = { id = germany_flavour_events.100 days = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

			modifier = {

					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }

					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }

country_event = { #Republic of Poland re-joins Reichspakt
	id = poland_events.225
	title = poland_events.225.t
	desc = poland_events.225.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.225 option poland_events.225.a"
		name = poland_events.225.a
		get_current_government_type = yes
		GER = {
			add_to_faction = POL
			set_autonomy = {
				target = POL
				autonomy_state = oststaat
				end_wars = no
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = german_research
			clr_country_flag = POL_forpol_wait
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_german_influence = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_trade_finished }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_polish_control }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_polish_control
					add_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
					add_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_german_cooperation }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_german_cooperation
					add_idea = POL_german_hegemony
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
					add_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = POL_german_hegemony
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
			POL_add_german_influence = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -5 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			set_country_flag = illusion_of_free_choice_achievement_condition
		}
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.235 option poland_events.235.a"
		name = poland_events.235.a
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 5 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		GAL_characters_join_poland_immediate = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = poland_flavour_events.29 days = 365 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland_events.236 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_former_faction_member }
				}
				GER = { country_event = poland_events.237 }
			}
			POL_transfer_popularity = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.25
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GAL = { exists = yes } }
				GAL = {
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = POL
						target_organization = 1
						source_organization = 1
						size = 0.6
						stockpile_ratio = 0.6
						army_ratio = 0.6
						air_ratio = 1
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		88 = { #Krakow
			add_core_of = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
				remove_core_of = AUS
			}
			transfer_state_to = ROOT
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_GAL_characters
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_polish_control }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_polish_control
				add_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_german_cooperation }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				add_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
				add_idea = POL_austrian_friendship
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
				add_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austrian_friendship }
			88 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			91 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else = { add_ideas = POL_austrian_cooperation }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { is_monarchy = no }
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 35 }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 20 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		AUS = { country_event = poland_events.246 }
	}
}

	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.243 option poland_events.243.a"
		name = poland_events.243.a

			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				tag = AUS
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
				GER_is_du_path = yes
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Polish_loyalty
				value = 10
				tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty < 1 }
					has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
				}
				activate_mission = GER_SPD_Polish_rift
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.243 option poland_events.243.b"
		name = poland_events.243.b
		trigger = {
			has_democratic_government = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				tag = AUS
				NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_GER }
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -15
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
				GER_is_du_path = yes
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Polish_loyalty
				value = 10
				tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty < 1 }
					has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
				}
				activate_mission = GER_SPD_Polish_rift
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
			POL = { country_event = poland_events.244 }
		}
	}

					has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
				POL = {
					is_ai = no
					has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				UKR = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				POL = {
					is_ai = no
					has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				UKR = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GAL }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = AUS_enacted_military_occupation }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					GAL = {
						every_core_state = {
							limit = {
								is_owned_by = GAL
								NOT = { state = 73 } #Transcarpathia
							}
							remove_claim_and_add_core_of_ROOT = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					GAL = {
						every_core_state = {
							limit = {
								is_owned_by = GAL
								NOT = { state = 73 } #Transcarpathia
							}
							add_claim_by = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				annex_country = {
					target = GAL
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		save_event_target_as = POL_UKR_everything
		UKR = { country_event = poland_events.248 }
		POL = { country_event = poland_events.249 } #Austria keeps it
	}
	option = { #Everything for Poland
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.246 option poland_events.246.c"
		name = poland_events.246.c
		trigger = {
			POL = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = POL_Krakow
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				POL = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
				OR = {
					UKR = {
						has_soclib_or_socdem_government = no
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
					}
					UKR = {
						has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				UKR = {
					has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				POL = {
					has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				UKR = { has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes }
			}
		}

	}

			}
		}

			}

					73 = { owner = { original_tag = AUS } } #Transcarpathia

				}

			}
			var:664.owner = { country_event = poland_events.258 } #Owner of Southern Slovakia
		}
	}
}

#Operation Parasol
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.259
	title = poland_events.259.t
	desc = poland_events.259.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_rydz
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.259 option poland_events.259.a"
		name = poland_events.259.a
		set_temp_variable = { stab_removal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
		add_to_temp_variable = { stab_removal = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
		divide_temp_variable = { stab_removal = -100 }
		add_stability = stab_removal
		set_temp_variable = { coup_strength = stab_removal }
		add_to_temp_variable = { coup_strength = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
		divide_temp_variable = { coup_strength = 200 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = coup_strength }
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = GER }
			GER = { end_puppet = POL }
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = poland_news_events.4
			POL_remove_guderian = yes
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = POL_paternal_autocrat2_party_long
				name = POL_paternal_autocrat2_party
			}
		}
		POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes
		POL_create_rydz = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = POL_Fill_The_Railway_Gaps }
			uncomplete_national_focus = { focus = POL_Fill_The_Railway_Gaps }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = POL_boguslaw_miedzinski_sic
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = POL_polish_lands
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			country_event = { id = poland_events.561 days = 14 }  #Economic crash
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = POL_revolt_from_monarchy }
				country_event = { id = poland_events.562 days = 97 } #King August Escapes
			}
			activate_mission = POL_reach_the_sea
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_national_committee } }
				RUS = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GER
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Demands
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.275
	title = poland_events.275.t
	desc = {
		text = poland_events.275.d.fra
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_INT_negotiations }
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland_events.275.d.rus
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_RUS_negotiations }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.275 option poland_events.275.a"
		name = poland_events.275.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_INT_negotiations }
		country_event = { id = poland_events.278 days = 14 }
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = poland_news_events.1 days = 15 }
		}
		remove_ideas = {
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_1
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_2
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_3
			POL_dawn_of_progress_psl_1
			POL_dawn_of_progress_psl_2
			POL_dawn_of_progress_psl_3
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_psl_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
			leave_faction = yes
			POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes
			POL_remove_guderian = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
				}
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { tag = ROOT }
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = ROOT
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
		}
		FRA = { add_to_faction = POL }
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { country_event = poland_events.276 }
			clr_country_flag = POL_INT_negotiations
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.275 option poland_events.275.a"
		name = poland_events.275.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_RUS_negotiations }
		country_event = { id = poland_events.279 days = 14 }
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = poland_news_events.2 days = 15 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
			leave_faction = yes
			POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes
			POL_remove_guderian = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
				}
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { tag = ROOT }
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = ROOT
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
		}
		MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
		leave_faction = yes
		RUS = { add_to_faction = POL }
		hidden_effect = {
			INT = { country_event = poland_events.276 }
			clr_country_flag = POL_RUS_negotiations
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.275 option poland_events.275.b"
		name = poland_events.275.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FROM = { country_event = poland_events.277 }
	}
}

#Poland gives in to the French
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.278
	title = poland_events.278.t
	desc = poland_events.278.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_revolution

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.278 option poland_events.278.a"
		name = poland_events.278.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_WK2_reparations }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = POL_WK2_reparations_fra
				days = 730
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = POL_Revolutionary_Republic
		if = {
			limit = { INT = { has_government = totalist } }
			promote_character = {
				character = POL_kazimierz_zakrzewski
				ideology = totalist_subtype
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			activate_advisor = POL_stanislaw_bukowiecki_sic
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = syndicalist
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			activate_advisor = POL_pawel_lew_marek_sic
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = totalist }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:totalist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_stability = -0.15
		POL_purge_right_generals = yes
		POL_return_rokossowski = yes
	}
}

			add_stability = -0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			POL = {
				set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -10 }
				POL_add_german_influence = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_du_path = yes
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = GER_Polish_loyalty
					value = 10
					tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_loss
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty < 1 }
						has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
					}
					activate_mission = GER_SPD_Polish_rift
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
	}

	}

country_event = {#Economic treaty between POL, GER and AUS
	id = poland_events.313
	title = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }
		text = poland_events.313.t.pol
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 50 } }
		text = poland_events.313.t.ger
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }
		text = poland_events.313.d.pol
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 50 } }
		text = poland_events.313.d.ger
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control0
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control1
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control2
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control3
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control4
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets0
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets1
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets2
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets3
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets4
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.313 option poland_events.313.a"
		name = poland_events.313.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }#poles control their economy
		add_ideas = POL_polish_control
		add_political_power = POL_influence
		set_temp_variable = { POL.POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = poland_events.314 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland_events.314 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.313 option poland_events.313.a"
		name = poland_events.313.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 50 } } #poles don't control
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { POL_GER_influence > 30 }
				check_variable = { POL_AUS_influence < 10 }
				GER = { exists = yes }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_german_cooperation
			set_temp_variable = { POL.POL_influence_change = 3 }
			POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes

			POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { POL_AUS_influence > 30 }
				check_variable = { POL_GER_influence < 10 }
				AUS = { exists = yes }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_austrian_cooperation
			set_temp_variable = { POL.POL_influence_change = 5 }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { AUS = { exists = yes } }
			add_ideas = POL_austro_german_condominium
		}
		else = { add_ideas = POL_german_cooperation }
	}
}

			}
		}

			set_autonomy = {
				target = POL

				end_wars = no
			}

			set_country_flag = POL_autonomy

		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.327 option poland_events.327.b"
		name = poland_events.327.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_elected_government = no
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			end_puppet = POL
		}
		POL = {
			set_country_flag = POL_independence
			country_event = poland_events.328
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.327 option poland_events.327.c"
		name = poland_events.327.c

		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_autonomy }
		text = poland_events.328.t2
	}
	desc = poland_events.328.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.328 option poland_events.328.a"
		name = poland_events.328.a
		get_current_government_type = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_autonomy }
			GER = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = POL
					autonomy_state = oststaat_autonomous
					end_wars = no
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = POL_autonomy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_independence }
			GER = { end_puppet = POL }
			clr_country_flag = POL_independence
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		if = {
			limit = { is_monarchy = yes }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = POL_kingdom } }
					set_cosmetic_tag = POL_kingdom
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_german_hegemony }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_german_hegemony
				add_idea = POL_polish_control
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_german_cooperation }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				add_idea = POL_polish_control
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
				add_idea = POL_polish_control
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = poland_events.332
	title = poland_events.332.t
	desc = poland_events.332.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_tp_tank

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.332 option poland_events.332.a"
		name = poland_events.332.a
		ai_chance = { base = 15 }
		FROM = {
			set_global_flag = POL_infantry_exercise
			country_event = poland_events.333
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.332 option poland_events.332.b"
		name = poland_events.332.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_tech = superior_firepower
					has_tech = grand_battle_plan
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_global_flag = POL_artillery_exercise
			country_event = poland_events.333
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.332 option poland_events.332.c"
		name = poland_events.332.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_army_size = {
					size > 3
					type = armor
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_tech = mobile_warfare
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_global_flag = POL_armour_exercise
			country_event = poland_events.333
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.332 option poland_events.332.e"
		name = poland_events.332.e
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
}

#lessons from the exercises
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.334
	title = poland_events.334.t
	desc = poland_events.334.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_tp_tank

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.334 option poland_events.334.a"
		name = poland_events.334.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_infantry_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_mobility_focus
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = motorized_equipment
				category = cat_mechanized_equipment
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { attack_skill_level < 10 }
				add_attack = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_infantry_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_mobility_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_infantry_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_communication_focus
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = recon_tech
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { logistics_skill_level < 10 }
				add_logistics = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_infantry_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_communication_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_infantry_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_concentration_focus
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = infantry_weapons
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { planning_skill_level < 10 }
				add_planning = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_infantry_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_concentration_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_artillery_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_mobility_focus
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				cost_reduction = 0.2
				uses = 1
				category = land_doctrine
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { attack_skill_level < 10 }
				add_attack = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_artillery_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_mobility_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_artillery_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_communication_focus
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = radar_tech
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { defense_skill_level < 10 }
				add_defense = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_artillery_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_communication_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_artillery_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_concentration_focus
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = artillery
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { planning_skill_level < 10 }
				add_planning = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_artillery_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_concentration_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_armour_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_mobility_focus
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = armor
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { logistics_skill_level < 10 }
				add_logistics = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_armour_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_mobility_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_armour_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_communication_focus
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = signal_company_tech
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { attack_skill_level < 10 }
				add_attack = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_armour_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_communication_focus
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = POL_armour_exercise
				has_global_flag = POL_concentration_focus
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				name = poland_events.334.t
				cost_reduction = 0.2
				uses = 1
				category = land_doctrine
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { planning_skill_level < 10 }
				add_planning = 1
			}
			clr_global_flag = POL_armour_exercise
			clr_global_flag = POL_concentration_focus
		}
		else = {
			army_experience = 25
		}
	}
}

	title = poland_events.352.t
	desc = poland_events.352.d

	desc = poland_events.353.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_scandal

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.353 option poland_events.353.a"
		name = poland_events.353.a
		add_stability = -0.06
		if = {
			limit = { is_monarchy = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -6 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -6 }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		}

country_event = {
	id = poland_events.374
	title = poland_events.374.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = yes }
		text = poland_events.374.d.dem
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = no }
		text = poland_events.374.d.nat
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.374 option poland_events.374.a"
		name = poland_events.374.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tag = ALB
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ALB_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = BUL
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = BUL_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = EST
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = EST_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = GRE
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GRE_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = BPL_dissolution option = BPL_DISSOLUTION_GRE_KEEP } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = LAT
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = LAT_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = SER
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = BPL_dissolution option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = UKR
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BPL
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		POL = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.374 option poland_events.374.b"
		name = poland_events.374.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tag = ALB
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ALB_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = BUL
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = BUL_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = EST
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = EST_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = GRE
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = GRE_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = BPL_dissolution option = BPL_DISSOLUTION_GRE_KEEP } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = LAT
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = LAT_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = SER
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = BPL_dissolution option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = UKR
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland_events.375 }
	}
}

					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
	}
}

#Nationalist Revolt - intro
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.410
	title = poland_events.410.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_monarchy = yes }
		text = poland_events.410.d.kingdom
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_monarchy = no }
		text = poland_events.410.d.republic
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_army_march

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = { set_country_flag = POL_nationalist_uprising }

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.410 option poland_events.410.a"
		name = poland_events.410.a
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = poland_events.411 days = 7 } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_monarchy = yes }
			set_country_flag = POL_revolt_from_monarchy
		}
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND REVOLTS - Nationalists"
	}
}

#Nationalist coup
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.411
	title = poland_events.411.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_monarchy = yes }
		text = poland_events.411.d.kingdom
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_monarchy = no }
		text = poland_events.411.d.republic
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_BUL_Zveno_Coup

	immediate = { POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes }

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.411 option poland_events.411.a"
		name = poland_events.411.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = poland_events.419
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.1
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		activate_advisor = POL_tadeusz_bielecki_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		POL_set_up_uprising = yes
		activate_mission = POL_military_takeover
		activate_mission = POL_sejm_revolt
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = poland_news_events.6
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_PATAUT }
					paternal_autocrat < 0.1
					POL = { is_ai = yes }
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.1
				}
			}
			POL_update_military = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = POL_Legacy_of_the_Legions
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = POL_purged_rydz
						has_character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly
					}
				}
				POL_create_rydz = yes
				POL_edward_rydz_smigly = {
					promote_leader = yes
					remove_unit_leader_trait = old_guard
					add_max_trait = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#The Strike turns into Revolution
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.413
	title = poland_events.413.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_monarchy = yes }
		text = poland_events.413.d.kingdom
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_monarchy = no }
		text = poland_events.413.d.republic
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_revolution

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes }

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.413 option poland_events.413.a"
		name = poland_events.413.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = poland_events.418
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.1
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = poland_news_events.5
		}
		activate_advisor = POL_pawel_lew_marek_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:totalist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_PPS_Dubois }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		POL_return_rokossowski = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = POL_totalist2_party_long
				name = POL_totalist2_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = POL_syndicalist3_party_long
				name = POL_syndicalist3_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = POL_radical_socialist3_party_long
				name = POL_radical_socialist3_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = POL_social_democrat3_party_long
				name = POL_social_democrat3_party
			}
			POL_update_military = yes
		}
		POL_set_up_uprising = yes
	}
}

#Warning event
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.420
	title = poland_events.420.t
	desc = poland_events.420.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		POL = {
			OR = {
				POL_syndicalist_revolution_trigger = yes
				POL_nationalist_uprising_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.420 option poland_events.420.a"
		name = poland_events.420.a
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { POL_syndicalist_revolution_trigger = yes } }
			set_country_flag = POL_revolt_warning_syndicalist
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { POL = { POL_nationalist_uprising_trigger = yes } }
			set_country_flag = POL_revolt_warning_nationalist
		}
	}
}

	id = poland_events.543
	title = poland_events.543.t
	desc = poland_events.543.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_german_officer

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		POL = { has_war_with = GER }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.543 option poland_events.543.a"
		name = poland_events.543.a
		trigger = { tag = POL }
		add_stability = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = GAL }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = POL_defections
				days = 110
			}
			hidden_effect = { GAL = { country_event = poland_events.543 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = POL_defections
				days = 110
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = POL_defections
				days = 70
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { GER = { country_event = poland_events.543 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.543 option poland_events.543.b"
		name = poland_events.543.b
		trigger = {
			tag = GAL
			has_war_with = POL
		}
		add_manpower = 2500
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.543 option poland_events.543.c"
		name = poland_events.543.c
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		add_manpower = 1200

#Massive Economic Crash
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.561
	title = poland_events.561.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 51 } }
		text = poland_events.561.d.a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }
		text = poland_events.561.d.b
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday
	trigger = { NOT = { has_idea = POL_polish_control } }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = POL_uprising_crash
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = POL_economic_restructuring_2 }
			}
			else = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = POL_economic_restructuring_1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.561 option poland_events.561.a"
		name = poland_events.561.a
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 51 } }
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash1
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash2
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.561 option poland_events.561.b"
		name = poland_events.561.b
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 51 } }
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash3
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash4
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.561 option poland_events.561.c"
		name = poland_events.561.c
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 51 } }
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash5
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash6
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	option = {

		name = poland_events.594.b #give them what they want

			base = 5

				}

				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_in_faction = no

country_event = {
	id = poland_events.604
	title = poland_events.604.t
	desc = poland_events.604.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_zakrzewski

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.604 option poland_events.604.a"
		name = poland_events.604.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader_with_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution } }
			add_country_leader_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = POL_kazimierz_zakrzewski
			ideology = totalist_subtype
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			long_name = POL_syndicalist3_party_long
			name = POL_syndicalist3_party
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		activate_advisor = POL_stanislaw_bukowiecki_sic
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.05 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = poland_events.606 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.604 option poland_events.604.b"
		name = poland_events.604.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution }
			remove_country_leader_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		country_event = { id = poland_events.607 days = 7 }
	}
}

#Governing the Eastern Regions
country_event = {
	id = poland_events.650
	title = poland_events.650.t
	desc = poland_events.650.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.650 option poland_events.650.a"
		name = poland_events.650.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 201 #Zhitomir
				owns_state = 206 #Minsk
				check_variable = { num_owned_states > 40 }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 201 #Zhitomir
				owns_state = 206 #Minsk
			}
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_any_state_of = {
					201 #Zhitomir
					206 #Minsk
				}
			}
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_2
		}
		else = { #only Lithuania
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_1
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core_of = POL }
				is_claimed_by = POL
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = POL_communes }
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		country_event = poland_events.651
		hidden_effect = { news_event = poland_news_events.8 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = poland_events.700
	title = poland_events.700.t
	desc = poland_events.700.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_trial_big

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.700 option poland_events.700.a"
		name = poland_events.700.a
		retire_character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly
		retire_character = POL_adam_koc
		retire_character = POL_waclaw_stachiewicz
		retire_character = POL_leon_berbecki
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GAL_wladyslaw_sikorski }
			GAL_wladyslaw_sikorski = { retire = yes }
		}
		retire_character = POL_kazimierz_sosnkowski
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.2 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_country_flag = POL_purged_rydz
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.700 option poland_events.700.b"
		name = poland_events.700.b
		army_experience = -20
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.05 }
		set_country_flag = POL_purged_rydz
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.700 option poland_events.700.c"
		name = poland_events.700.c
		add_political_power = -60
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.1 }
		clear_army_chief = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly } }
			POL_create_rydz = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = POL_edward_rydz_smigly_army_chief
		add_trait = {
			character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly
			slot = army_chief
			trait = POL_marshal_of_the_nation
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
				character = POL_edward_rydz_smigly
				value = no
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_unable_to_remove_tt
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		remove_mission = POL_military_takeover
	}
}

	id = poland_events.801
	title = {
		trigger = { GER = { is_monarchy = yes } }
		text = poland_events.801.t.kaiser
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { GER = { is_monarchy = no } }
		text = poland_events.801.t
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { GER = { is_monarchy = yes } }
		text = poland_events.801.d.kaiser
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { GER = { is_monarchy = no } }
		text = poland_events.801.d
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_army_march

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		is_monarchy = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_alex_not_heir }
		has_character = POL_alexander_von_hohenzollern
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event poland_events.801 option poland_events.801.a"
		name = poland_events.801.a
		86 = { transfer_state_to = POL }
		67 = { transfer_state_to = POL }
		hidden_effect = {
			add_state_core = 86
			add_state_core = 67
			GER = { end_puppet = POL }
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				set_country_flag = how_its_made_achievement_condition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { GER = { is_monarchy = yes } }
			add_country_leader_trait = POL_the_kaiser_maker
			hidden_effect = {
				var:country_leader = {
					set_character_flag = POL_the_kaiser_maker
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { GER = { is_monarchy = no } }
			add_country_leader_trait = POL_last_hohenzollern
			hidden_effect = {
				var:country_leader = {
					set_character_flag = POL_last_hohenzollern
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #donotlog debug event to log the path that Poland is on at 1.1.1939
	id = poland_events.999
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = KR.hidden.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = market_liberal }
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND GOVERNMENT Market Liberal"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND GOVERNMENT Authoritarian Democrat"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND GOVERNMENT Social Conservative"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND GOVERNMENT Social Liberal/Social Democrat"
		}
	}
}

	}

		trigger = {

			POL = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz } }
		}
	}
	desc = {

		}

		trigger = { original_tag = AUS }
	}

	option = {
		name = poland_news_events.12.c # Other Reichspakt
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = GER }
			is_in_faction_with = GER
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland_news_events.12.e # Socialists
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = poland_news_events.12.f # Russia and allies
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = RUS
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
			}
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland_news_events.12.g # Generic
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			NOT = { original_tag = AUS }
			NOT = { original_tag = RUS }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = RUS }
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}
}
